ALARM & ERROR LIST (ALARM A)

1071Memory board / battery hurry exchange
       The memory board battery has finished its service life.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
        Battery in the memory board
       [Measures to Take]
        Replace the battery in the memory board.
1089PLC alarm No. illegal
       The PLC requested an alarm number outside the setting
       range.
       [Code]XYYYY
        X:Requested alarm level
         A->Request of alarm A
         B->Request of alarm B
         C->Request of alarm C
         D->Request of alarm D
        YYYY:Requested alarm number in hexadecimal
1091PLC alarm message file not load
       The PLC alarm message file is not found, disabling normal
       alarm processing.
       [Code] 
        PLC alarm message file loading status (hexadecimal)
        1-> End of file was received without loading any character.
        3-> End of file was received during file loading.
        9-> The device name was wrongly specified.
        A-> The file name was wrongly specified.
        B-> The file was not found.
1092PLC backup data file load
       Backup copy onto the PLC backup file failed.
       [Code] XXXXYYYY
        XXXX->Backup processing error status
        YYYY->Backup cycle number
1093PLC backup data file not load
       The PLC backup data file is not found, disabling backup
       processing.
       [Code]
        PLC backup data file loading status (hexadecimal)
        1  -> End of file was received without loading any character.
        3  -> End of file was received during file loading.
        9  -> The device name was wrongly specified.
        A  -> The file name was wrongly specified.
        B  -> The file was not found.
        100-> Wrong PLC machine type
        200-> Wrong PLC class
        300-> Wrong file version
1094PLC back up data file reading
       PLC back up data file does not read from memory.
       [Code] XXX
        2  ->file open errors (file none)
        3  ->file read errors (data none)
        4  ->file attribute errors ('PBU1' be)
        5  ->file close errors
        6  ->file size errors (file size small)
        7  ->file size errors (file size big)
        100->A machine type of PLC differs.
        200->A class of PLC differs.
        300->File version differs.
1097Safety Speed Monitor error
       Concerning check processing of Safety-Speed-Monitor
       at the time of guard-close of production mode, error
       signal of Safety-Speed-Monitor did not turn ON after
       the specific time.
       Or, NC was informed of mode of production-setting-test
       which does not exist.
       [Code] X
        1->Concerning check processing of Safety-Speed-Monitor
           at the time of guard-close of production mode, error
           signal of Safety-Speed-Monitor did not turn it on once
           within a specific time.
        2->NC was informed of mode of production-setting-test
           which does not exist.
       [Probable Faulty Location]
        1)Safety-Speed-Monitor or PLC software,Data-file for
          Safety-Speed-Monitor
        2)Safety-Speed-Monitor or PLC software
1098MCS operation ready off
       MCS operation ready turns off.
       [Object] Axis
       [Code] X
        Power supply unit status
        bit7:PSRDY  PSRDY input is ON.
        bit6:PSRSTS This signal turns ON when PSRDY input turns ON.
        .	     This signal turns OFF when PSRDY input turns OFF.
        .	     After reset sequence this signal turns ON again.
        bit5:OPRON  OPRON input is ON.
        bit4:PWON   PWON input is ON.
        bit3:DC power ON(DCON) DC power is being supplied.
        bit2:Operation command bit(DRV)
        bit1:Not used
        bit0:Not used
1100Reset machine data 
       The backup data caused an error and the factory-set
       initial data was forciby loaded. Machine data must be
       set again.
       [Object]
        None
       [Character-string]
        None
       [Code] XXXXYYYY
        XXXX
          bit 0:SPARE
          bit 1:HD backup status file
          bit 2:Low speed NC backup data file
          bit 3:High speed NC backup data file
          bit 4:PLC backup data file
          bit 5:PLC-HMI data file
          bit 6:Alarm history data file
          bit 7:PLC axis data file
          bit 8:POT TOOL data file(M/C only)
          bit 9:MOP TOOL data file(M/C only)
          bit10:MOP TOOL Parameter file(M/C only)
        YYYY
          1:File read open error
          2:File read error
          3:Version check error
          4:Check sum error
          5:Double check sum error
          6:Backup memory check error
          7:File write open error
          8:File write error

       [Object]

1104DeviceNet slave idle mode 
       DeviceNet slave station was in idle condition.
       [Object]
       None
       [Character-string]
       CH*SC$
        *:Channel number where the error occurred
        $:Sequence counter
       [Code]
       XXYYZZZZ
       XX MacID of idle condition slave station
       YY Error status of slave station XX
        0x00:Normal or nonexistent slave station
        0x46:Duplicate MacID error
        0x48:Communication stop
        0x49:Discrimination information was not compatible with
             scan list
        0x4D:Data size not compatible with scan list
        0x4E:No response in the connection check
        0x4F:Other slave stations are nonexistence on network
        0x50:Idle mode condition
        0x53:Error received in the connection check
        0x54:Timeout occurred in the connection check
        0x56:Turn into idle mode
        0x5B:Bus off
        0x5C:Network power supply off
         (XXYY become 0xFFFF,if its not caused by slave station,
         such as communication delay.)
       ZZZZ:Scanner error status
        bit0:Memory check error(when memory initialized)
        bit1:Scan list initialize error
        bit2:Scan list mismatch error(MacID)
        bit3:Scan list mismatch error(Input data)
        bit4:Scan list mismatch error(output data)
        bit5:Duplicate MacID error
        bit6:Network power supply status error
        bit7:Memory parity error
        bit8:Input data reception error(single)
        bit9:Input data reception error(double)
        bit10:Output data transmission error(single)
        bit11:Output data transmission error(double)
        bit12:Slave station communication delay error(single)
        bit13:Slave station communication delay error(double)
        bit14:Bus off
        bit15:Diagnostic information access error
       [ Probable Faulty Locations ]
       1.Hardware failure
       2.Software failure
1105DTL error 
       A DTL error was detected.
       [Object]
       None
       [ Probable Faulty Locations ]
       1.Software failure
1106FL-net initial error 
       An error occurred during initialization of FL-net.
       [Object]
       None
       [Character-string]
       None
       [Code]
       None
       [ Probable Faulty Locations ]
       FL-net communication parameters are wrong.
       [ Measures to Take]
       Start up the FL-net Monitor tool and check the initial 
       parameter data.
       Then, set the correct communication parameters before 
       restarting the FL-net.
1107Important illegal 
       A serious error occurred during startup of the FL-net card.
       [Object]
       None
       [Character-string]
       None
       [Code]
       Y000XXXX
       When Y=0, XXXX=7F00 System error
       	       7F01 Flash memory error
       	       7F02 DRAM test error
       	       7F03 NICE test error
       	       7F04 EEPROM sum check error
       	       7F05 CPU BUS error
       	       7F06 Illegal instruction
       If Y=1, XXXX = 4000. Timeout error of 4 sec or longer
       If Y=2, XXXX : CommonMemory busy count
           When Y=3, XXXX=State of self node
       		bit 3: Double detection of common memory 
       		       bit address
       		bit 4: Double detection of common memory 
       		       word address
       		bit 6: Token monitor timeout error
       		bit 7: Double detection of self node number
       [ Probable Faulty Locations ]
       FL-net card is defective.
1108Non-answered software was detected
       [Object]
       None
       [Character-string]
       None
       [Code]
       It means a name of Non-answered software by ASCII.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       NC software
1109The error occurred while CAS works 
       A virtual machine is controlled with the CAS software. 
       The error occurred by processing this CAS software. 
       Under such a condition, the processing of the interference 
       detection and the model display, etc. is not done
       [Character-string]
       None
       [Code]
       The return value from the CAS software is indicated.
       [ Expected faulty point ]
       Abnormality and the damage, etc. of 3D model data are 
       thought. 
       [ Treatment measures ]
       The collision avoidance function is invalid though the
       pulsefeed in the state to push "Interlock release" button
       is possible  by the deletion of the alarm by NC reset even
       if this alarm  is generated. 
       It is necessary to turn on the power supply again once 
       to make the collision avoidance function effective. 
       Please inquire of our service if the phenomenon relapses.

1121PSC Optical scale encoder error
       An error was detected by the position encoder of optical scale.
       [Character-string]None
       [Code]XXYYZZ
       XX:Value of the J-type endoder and value of the optical scale
          are too different.
         bit1:It is too different by a negative sign.
         bit0:It is too different by a positive sign.
       YY:Pulse count value of optical scale
         bit0:A-phase pulse and B-phase pulse have changed at the same
         time.
       ZZ:The amplitude of the optical scale signal is wrong.
         bit1:The amplitude of B-phase is wrong.
         bit0:The amplitude of A-phase is wrong.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - Breakdown of optical scale
       - Breakdown of optical scale cable
       [Measures to Take]
       - Exchange of optical scale
       - Exchange of optical scale cables

1123Safety speed monitor error
       An error occurred in the safety speed monitor.
       [Object]None
       [Character-string]None
       [Code]
       0x61XX0000->Speed over
         XX=Axis number of the target axis
       0x62XX0000->Parameter setting error
         XX=Axis number of the target axis
       0x63XX0000->Machine operation mode error
         XX=Axis number of the target axis
       0x64XXYYYY->Safety position frame diagnosis error (Encoder axis)
         XX=Axis number of the target axis
         YY=Error information from safety speed monitor
           bit11->Refresh check error
           bit10->CRC error
           bit9 ->Safety frame CRC error
           bit4 ->Excitation stop was detected
           bit3 ->CPU error
           bit2 ->Pulse count error
           bit1 ->Modulation code error
           bit0 ->Source address or destination address error
       0x65XXYYYY->Safety position frame diagnosis error
       		 (Magnet encoder / PG axis)
         XX=Axis number of the target axis
         YY=Error information from safety speed monitor
           bit7 ->Actual speed was mismatch between counter 1
       		  and counter 2
           bit4 ->CRC error
           bit3 ->Refresh check 2 error
           bit2 ->Refresh check 1 error
           bit1 ->Counter 2 pulse input error
           bit0 ->Counter 1 pulse input error
       0x66XX0000->Axis exchanging error
         XX=Axis number of the target axis
       0x67XX0000->Stop monitoring displacement distance over
         XX=Axis number of the target axis
       0x68XX0000->Max speed over 
         XX=Axis number of the target axis
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
        - Safety speed monitor
        - Safety speed monitor data file
1132VDU communication error
       An error occurred in the VDU(Vibration Detect Unit)
       communication link, disabling the VDU 
       from detecting acceleration.
       [Object]Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string]NONE
       [Code]XXYYZZZZ
       XX = FF [HEX] (fixed)
       YY = 00 [HEX] (fixed)
       ZZZZ = VDU link error status at the time of error detection.
       (Each bit represents the kind of communication error.)
        bit 15 Undefined
        bit 14 Undefined
        bit 13 Undefined
        bit 12 1: Error in communication with VDU(AT mode)
        bit 11 1: Error in communication with VDU(MT mode)
        bit 10 1: Transmission loop error in AT (auto) mode
        bit 9	1: Data over error in data receiving part of interface
        bit 8	Undefined
        bit 7	Undefined
        bit 6	1: Modulation code error
        bit 5	1: CRC error
        bit 4	1: Format error
        bit 3	1: Double transmission error
        bit 2	1: Double reception error
        bit 1	1: Modulation code error
        bit 0	1: Time-out error
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - VDU
       - Encoder link cables
       - VFA unit
1133VDU error
       The VDU(Vibration Detect Unit) has become unable to
       detect acceleration data. 
       [Object]Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string]NONE
       [Code]XXYYZZZZ
       XX = VDU error status
        bit7	1: Error bit (1 is error)
        bit6	1: Empty bit
        bit5	1: Latest acceleration data is overflow(Y axis)
        bit4	1: Latest acceleration data is overflow(X axis)
        bit3	1: Empty bit
        bit2	1: Error in communication
       (toggled detecting each error)
        bit1	1: Previous acceleration data is overflow(Y axis)
        bit0	1: Previous acceleration data is overflow(X axis)
       YY = VDU alarm code
        01: Stop command halt
        02: Control parameter error
        07: User parameter check sum error
        0E: Synchronous miss error
        15: Acceleration sensor signal error (X axis)
        16: Acceleration sensor signal error (Y axis)
        17: Acceleration sensor signal error (X and Y axis)
       ZZZZ= 0 (fixed)
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - VDU
1134VDU initialize failed
       An error occurred in initialization of
       VDU(Vibration Detect Unit).
       [Object]Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string]NONE
       [Code]XXYYZZZZ
       XX = Encoder link sequence number
            at the time of error detection
        0: Reset
        1: Network address setting
        2: Request of basic information on communication
        3: Change of communication version
        4: Acquisition of device information
        5: Parameter change
        6: AT (auto) mode start
       YY = Error content
        0: Communication error
        1: Transmission start time over
        2: Transmission finishes time over
        3: Reception finishes time over
        4: Abnormal response address
        5: Abnormal response code
        6: Parameter error
       ZZZZ = Additional data
        If YY=0,
         the encoder link error status C2ERR at the
         time of error detection appears.
        If YY=1, 2, or 3,
         the transferred frame information C2MTINF appears.
        If YY=4,
         the network address of the responding device appears.
        If YY=5,
         the received frame information C2RXINF appears.
        If YY=6,
         the number of parameter that caused the alarm appears.
          1 = Not all the necessary parameters are received.
          2 = Basic information on communication is incompatible.
          4 = Protocol version on communication is incompatible.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - VDU
       - Encoder link cables
       - VFA unit
1135MCS DD Encoder-link error
       An error occurred in the encoder communication link.
       [Object]
        Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string]
        None
       [Code] XXYYZZZZ
        XX = $FF (fixed)
        YY = $00: Error is detected at the DD encoder.
             $01: Error is detected at the 
       		 DD encoder(slave sensor).
        ZZZZ = Encoder link error status at the
       			      time of error detection
       	bit15: Undefined
       	bit14: Undefined
       	bit13: Error in communication with the DD encoder
       		(slave sensor)
       	bit12: Error in communication with the DD encoder
       	bit11: MT buffer error
       	bit10: Transmission loop error in AT mode
       	bit9 : Data over error in data receiving part of
       	       interface
       	bit8 : Undefined
       	bit7 : Undefined
       	bit6 : Modulation code error
       	bit5 : CRC error
       	bit4 : Format error
       	bit3 : Double transmission error
       	bit2 : Double reception error
       	bit1 : Parity error
       	bit0 : Time-out error
        This alarm occurs only at ICB-H.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
        DD encoder of DD encoder (slave sensor) of the pertinent axis
        Encoder link cables or connectors
        Inverter unit control board
1136MCS DD Encoder error
       The DD encoder has become undetectable.
       [Object]
        Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string]
        None
       [Code] XXYYZZZZ
        XX = Positional data status
             bit7  : Error bit (1:error)
             bit6  : Absolute position sensor margin error
             .       (0:Normal, 1:Warning)
             bit5  : Gap-Warning (1:Gap-small,Toggle:Gap-big)
             bit4  : Inclination-Warning (1:CCW-big, Toggle:CW-big)
             bit3  : Auto set mode (0:Normal, 1:Auto mode)
             bit2  : Communication error (Toggle by detecting)
             bit1,0: Error bit number of absolute position code
             .       (It is indicated by 2bits.)
        YY = Alarm code
             01: Stop command has stopped.
             02: Control parameter error
             04: Absolutization error
             05: Initialization speed too high
             08: Auto-set-data error
             0D: Speed too high
             0E: Synchronization error
             20: Absolutization mismatch (Only Format-5)
             21: Communication-error of Master-sensor (Only Format-5)
             3E: Code-error by Absolute-position-sensor
             3F: Check-errotr by Absolute-position-code
             40: Inclination-error (for plus)
             41: Inclination-error (for minus)
             42: Gap is narrow
             43: Gap is wide
        ZZZZ = 0000 fixed
        This alarm occurs only at ICB-H.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
        DD encoder

1138MCS DD Encoder initialize failed
       An error occurred in the initialization of the DD encoder.
       [Object]
       Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string]
       None
       [Code] XXYYZZZZ
        XX = Encoder link initialization sequence number (1B) 
             at the time of the error detection
              0: Reset
              1: Network address setting
              2: Request to send the basic information for communication
              3: Change of communication software version
              4: Acquisition of device information
              5: Parameter change
              6: Position detection start
              7: AT mode start
        YY = Error content (1B)
              0: Communication error
              1: Transmission start time over
              2: Transmission finish time over
              3: Reception finish time over
              4: Abnormal response address
              5: Abnormal response code
              6: Parameter error
        ZZZZ = Data (2B)
          If YY = 0,
             The encoder link error status C2ERR at the time of error
             detection appears.
          If YY = 1, 2 or 3,
             The transmitted frame information QC2MTINF appears.
          If YY = 4,
             The network address of the responding device appears.
          If YY = 5,
             Alarm code + positional data status
             Refer to MCS DD Encoder error (alarm 1136).
          If YY = 6,
             Parameter number at which the error is detected
              1: Reception of insufficient number of parameters
              2: Basic information for communication being incompatible
              3: Multi-turn detection range over
              4: Communication protocol version being incompatible
              5: Positional data format being incompatible
              6: Abbreviated data mode being incompatible
        However, when abnormal voltage is detected at the encoder fuse
          XXYY = $FFFF fixed
          ZZZZ = Detected voltage value of the encoder fuse
       	  (12[V] = $9980)
       	  Normal range: 10.6[V] to 13.8[V]
       	  Allowable range: $8800 to $B000
        This alarm occurs only at ICB-H.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
        DD encoder
        Encoder link cables and connectors
        Inverter unit control board

1144MCS Power Supply Unit over load

       it surpassed W axis torque set data Z axis motor torque
       has set on a systematic parameter by a tailstook
       connection condition.
       As it clamped, it was about to move tailstook.

       1) Slide resistance of tailstook Z axis direction is big.
       2) Tailstook is clamped.

       "#11"-> Voltage drop of 5 V battery for control board
       "#12"-> Invertor bridge shorted
       "#13"-> IPM protective function activated
       "#14"-> Motor overcurrent
       "#20"-> INT loop error
       "#21"-> INT5 loop error
       "#22"-> INT4 loop error
       "#23"-> INT3 loop error
       "#24"-> INT2 loop error
       "#25"-> INT1 loop error
       "#26"-> Access denied
       "#27"-> Ram check error in initialization
       "#28"-> Party error

       "#30"-> IRQ7 interruption
       "#31"-> NMI interruption
       "#32"-> General illegal command
       "#33"-> Slot illegal command
       "#34"-> CPU address error
       "#35"-> DMA address error

1153MCS CON APA deviation
       Difference between CON and APA values has exceeded the
       allowable limit. The CON-APC deviation is the absolute
       value of difference between [calculated value written 
       in MCS] and [actual position read from MCS]. 
       The NC control software monitors this deviation. 
       The MCS normally monitors DIFF value.
       This alarm appears if the MCS causes a fatal error and
       cannot monitor the DIFF value.
       [Object] Axis name
       [Character-string] None
       [Code]
       Absolute value of deviation in hexadecimal (reference
       unit)
       [Probable Faulty Locations]

       - Mismatch between MCS data and NC data

       	signal status: 0)

        bit0 1:PWON input is closed.

       						[3.1V]

1179MCS CON speed over
       Increments for positioning command (SRCOND) issued from
       the NC to the invertor unit exceed the allowable limit.
       If this alarm occurs in the axis to be positioned, the
       servo data file has wrong data. (This is because the
       invertor unit calculates the increments for the axis to
       be positioned.)
       [Object] Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string] None
       [Code]
       Absolute value of increments processed for acceleration/
       deceleration [(pr/65536)/Tp]
       Where, pr= One turn of position encoder; Tp= Position
       control frequency
       The following codes, however, have specific meanings:
       1: The increments were so large that they were judged
          erroneous in preliminary check.
       2: The position command (SRCON) exceeds the absolute
          value of the encoder measuring range (linear axis only).
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - Servo data file
       - NC software
1180MCS Speed command over
       Speed command value issued from the NC to the invertor
       unit exceeds the allowable limit.
       [Object] Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string] None
       [Code] Speed command [(rev/4294967269)/Tv]
       rev= One motor turn; Tv= Speed control frequency
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - Servo data file
       - NC software
1181MCS DIFF over
       Axis movement caused a large positioning error.
       While the axis is in a target position or stopped, the
       target value and the calculated value are the same. 
       With an axis movement command, the NC starts creating
       calculation values (RCON) until the target point is
       reached. At this time, the actual position follows the
       calculated value with a certain delay. 
       This delay is called "following error" and calculated
       by ([calculation value] - [actual value]). 
       If the "following error" exceeds the allowable limit,
       the above alarm occurs.
       [Object] Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string] None
       [Code] Absolute value of following error [pr/65536]
       pr = One turn of position encoder
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - Overload due to faulty ball screw or bearing
       - Motor
       - Invertor unit
       - Servo data file
1182MCS APA speed over
       The position encoder value (RAPA) changes as the motor
       rotates. The NC checks this change with preset frequency.
       This alarm occurs if the change per unit time exceeds the
       allowable range consecutively. For example, an axis feedrate 
       is abnormally high compared with the normal rapid feedrate, 
       or the encoder value changes irregularly due to malfunction
       of the position encoder.
       [Object] Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string] None
       [Code]
       Absolute value of the change in encoder value per 
       position control frequency 
       [encoder's 1/65536 turn/position control frequency]
       The following codes, however, have specific meanings:
       1= Linear axis has exceeded its travel range.
       2= Rotary axis has exceeded its travel range (360) or
          limited axis has negative positional data.
       3= Limited axis has exceeded its travel range.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - Motor encoder (BL motor)
       - Encoder link cables or connectors (BL motor)
       - PG or magnetic encoder (VAC motor)
       - PG or magnetic encoder cables or connectors (VAC motor)
       - Invertor unit control board
1183MCS Full-closed APA error
       Difference between the full-closed loop encoder value
       and the motor encoder value exceeds the allowable range.
       [Object] Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string] None
       [Code] Number of times the error has been detected
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - Synthetic offset data is not set at the full-closed
         loop encoder or wrong data is set.
       - ABSO SCALE or position encoder with shaft
       - Excessive lost motion in axis drive system (The motor
         is not rigidly connected with the movable part.)
       - Slippage or breakage of shaft belt
       - Loose coupling between motor and ball screw
       - Improper positional loop gain (too high)
1184MCS Over speed
       Actual motor speed is too high.
       [Object] Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string] None
       [Code] Motor speed detected when this alarm occurred
              [(rev/4294967296)/Tv]
       Where, rev= One motor turn; Tv= Speed control frequency
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - Motor encoder (BL motor)
       - Encoder link cables or connectors (VAC motor)

1185MCS Velocity deviation over
       Actual motor speed excessively deviates from the speed
       command.
       [Object] Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string] None
       [Code] XXXXYYYY
       XXXX: Detected torque (sum of the torque data collected 
             for 3.2 ms)
          +-2^-12[MAXTRQ]
          If Tv = 0.4 ms, the momentary maximum torque is H'7FFF.
          If Tv = 0.8 ms, the momentary maximum torque is H'3FFF.
       YYYY: Detected acceleration (average value measured for 
             3.2 ms)
          +-2^-16[vr/3.2 ms/3.2 ms]
          = about 0.1 [1/min/ms]
       The code number 00000001 means that the error data is
       replaced by zero because of exponent underflow.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - The motor does not turn because of (mechanical lock or)
         application of large load.

        0: Reset
        1: Net address setting
        2: Request to send the basic information for 
           communication
        3: Change of communication software version
        4: Acquisition of device information
        5: Parameter change
        6: AT mode start
       YY-> Alarm content
        0: Communication error
        1: Transmission start time over
        2: Transmission end time over
        3: Reception end time over
        4: Wrong response address
        5: Wrong response code
        6: Parameter error
       ZZZZ-> Data
        YY = 0: Encoder link error status C2ERR established
       	on detection of the error
        YY = 1, 2, or 3: Transmitted frame information QC2MTINF
        YY = 4: Net address of the corresponding device
        YY = 5: Received frame information QC2RXINF
        YY = 6: Parameter number at which the error is detected
         1 = Reception of insufficient number of parameters
         2 = Basic information for communication being 
             incompatible
         3 = Multi-turn detection range over

1191MCS APA error
       An error occurred during calculation of APA value.
       [Object] Axis name or none (spindle)
       [Character-string] None
       [Code] XXXXXXXX
       1: Linear axis divided travel over
       2: Overflow during conversion of semi-position from
          [pr] to [pf].
       3: Underflow in synthesizing the axis data
       4: Overflow in synthesizing the axis data
       5: Overflow of input values used for hybrid control
       6: Overflow during initialization for hybrid control
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       - Motor encoder, encoder with shaft, or ABSO SCALE
       - Invertor unit control board
       - Servo data file
       If the alarm code is "1" or "3", the position encoder
       may not be properly offset to zero.
       If the alarm code is "4", the servo data file may be 
       defective.
       If the alarm code is "5" or "6", the motor coupling, 
       encoder with shaft, or ABSO SCALE may be loosely mounted.

         5: Parameter change

       But,in the case that voltage of encoder-fuse is failed,

1200Stroke end over
       An axis has hit the stroke end limit.
       [Code]
       None->The turret has hit the stroke end limit by X- or
       Z-axis command.
       1->During Y-axis movement on the machine with Y-axis
          function, the X-axis hit the stroke end limit.
       2->An axis hit the stroke end limit by M273 HP command
          (home position command within the stroke end limits).
       4->Present location (APA) exceeded the stroke end limit.
          Or, the stroke end limit was set internally in present
          location.
         (When the stroke end limit is set for the first time,
          it is generated without fail.)
       5->C-axis stroke over range in C-axis multi rev mode.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1->Operation error, programming error
       2->Setting error of soft-limit positions(positive/negative).
          (The soft-limit position is set outside the stroke end
           limit position.)
       3->Check the stroke end limit switches.
          (Is it turned on by chips or other foreign matter?)
       [Measures to Take]
       Push the reset button in the manual mode while turning
       on the emergency limit release switch on the control box,
       then move the turret away from the emergency limit
       position by rotating the pulse handle.
       After the emergency limit switch has been released, turn
       off the emergency limit release switch in the original
       position and re-set the soft-limit position.
       In the case of new LT control specification, it is moved
       an axis in the direction which goes away from stroke end
       limit.
1202Plus variable limit over
       An axis movement command to move the axis beyond the
       variable limit position in the positive direction is
       designated.
       [Object]AXIS
       [Code]
       1->In G00, G01, G32, G33, G34 or G35 mode
       2->In G02 or G03 mode; when restarting from manual
          interruption
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Axis command error (a value exceeding the variable
         limit in the positive direction has been specified)
       2)Setting error of the variable limit in the positive
         direction (set by user parameter)
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Correct the axis command value so that the target point
         does not exceed the variable limit in the positive 
         direction.
       2)Change the variable limit in the positive direction so
         that the target point of the specified axis command
         falls within a movable travel range.
       3)Check the tool offset value.
       4)Check the zero offset value.

       variable limit position in the negative direction is
       designated.

       2->In G02 or G03 mode; when restarting from manual
          interruption
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Axis command error (a value exceeding the variable
         limit in the negative direction has been specified)
       2)Setting error of the variable limit in the negative
         direction (set by user parameter)
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Correct the axis command value so that the target point
         does not exceed the variable limit in the negative 
         direction.
       2)Change the variable limit in the negative direction so
         that the target point of the specified axis command
         falls within a movable travel range.
       3)Check the tool offset value.
       4)Check the zero offset value.

1215S.M command asynchronous
       Under simultaneous four-axis control mode, S or M command
       provided with constant cutting speed code does not match
       between turret A and B for 2-saddle specification.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       Character-string:Coordinate system for G140, G141, or G142
       [Code]
       1->Mismatch of constant cutting speed codes (G96 and G97)
       2->Mismatch of turret selection commands (G110 and G111)
       3->Mismatch of S commands
       4->Mismatch of spindle rotation commands (M03, M04 and M05)
       5->Mismatch of spindle drive gear range commands
          (M40 through M44)
       6->Mismatch of M00 and M01
       7->Mismatch of M19 command
       8->Mismatch of M110 and M109
       9->M271, M272 instructions are different.
       10->M371, M372 instructions are different.
       11->M142, M143 instructions are different.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Mismatching S and/or M code command in simultaneous 
       four-axis cut program.
       Program Example:
        Turret A
         N100 G00 X500 Z500
         N101 M41 M03 S100 P10
        Turret B
         N200G00X500Z500
         N201M42M03S500P10
       	    ^^^^
       [Measures to Take]Correct the program.
       Example
       In the program above, change the commands in N201 sequence
       as indicated below:
         N201M41M03S100P10
       	    ^^^^
       Always designate the same S and M code commands at both
       turrets.
       [Related Specifications]2S specification
1216Synchronous P code
       P code commands are not designated in the ascending order
       for 2-saddle specification (except when the P commands are
       negative values).
       Or P commands for both A- and B-turrets have negative and
       mismatching values.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]
       1->There is a P command assigned with a numerical value
          smaller than the one assigned to the presently executed 
          P command.
       2->Mismatch between negative values of P commands for 
          A- and B-turrets.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]Program error
         G00X500Z500P30
         M41M03S500P20
       [Measures to Take]Correct the program.
       In the example, change P20 into P40 so that P code values
       increase orderly.

1221Duplicate M-code
       Before the execution of an M code, another M code which
       belongs to the same M-code group is designated (M07/M08, 
       and so forth).
       (In the case of process-combined machining such as thread
       cutting, this error occurs when the program is read and
       stored in the buffer.)
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Character-string]Designated M-code group
       ("M08" is displayed in the case of M08/M09.)
1222Interrupt return pointer unmatch
       After manual operation intervention to retract the cutting
       tool, the tool is returned to a different block from the
       block where the interruption was made. This alarm occurs
       when the number of execution blocks differs between the
       cycle starting after the reset and the sequence restart
       operation.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       The program contains a conditional statement which changes
       the number  of sequences to be executed. The conditional 
       statement is judged by whether the conditional expression 
       is true or the local variable is defined.
       Program Example:
        N0018 IF ABCD N0020
        N0019 ABCD=1 <- This defines the local variable.
        N0020
       In the first execution of the program, sequence N0019 is
       executed because there is no local variable ABCD. 
       In the sequence restart operation, however, sequence N0019
       is not executed.
       Related SpecificationTool retraction cycle
1223Thread feed
       In cutting a variable lead thread, the lead is zero or a
       negative value.
       Calculation error has occurred in the calculation of feed
       for variable lead thread cutting.
       [Object]AXIS, SYSTEM
       [Code]XX->Floating point calculation error
        Will convert to binary number.
             --X--   --X--
        bit 7 6 5 4 3 2 1 0			       HEX
        bit0->Overflow in converting into integer------01
        bit1->Exponential underflow--------------------02
        bit2->Exponential overflow---------------------04
        bit3->Calculation of root of a negative number-08
        bit4->Division by 0----------------------------10
        bit5->Angle overflow---------------------------20
       The codes indicated above are generated when calculation
       becomes impossible during thread lead calculation processing.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]Wrong F and E commands in the
       variable lead thread cutting command
       Program Example:
        G00  X100  Z100
        G33  X50   Z50  E-5  F10
       Feed becomes a negative value with the program indicated
       above.

       or G103.

       [Code]XYY
       YY:
        Bit0->Overflow in converting into integer
        Bit1->Exponential underflow
        Bit2->Exponential overflow
        Bit3->Calculation of root of a negative number
        Bit4->Division by 0
        Bit5->Angle overflow for SIN, COS, TAN and COT
       X:

        3->Former half of G102 (G103) tool path generation

        4->Latter half of G102 (G103) tool path generation

1259Tow-along tailstock connect
       G02, G03, G30, G31, G32, G33, G34, or G35 is designated
       while the tow-along tailstock body is connected. Or with
       the simple tow-along tailstock specification, an axis move
       command or turret indexing command is designated while
       the tailstock body is connected.
       [Code]
       None->An illegal G code is designated while the tow-along
             tailstock body is connected.
       2->With the simple tow-along specification, axis movement
          or turret indexing is attempted while the tailstock
          body is connected.
       3->In the automatic or MDI mode of operation,an axis
          move command is designated while the tailstock body 
          is connected.
       4->The tow-along tailstock connection command was issued
          in the Y-axis control mode.
       5->In tow-along tailstook concatenaion, home position
          translocation instruction (OGL) was performed.
       6->In self-travelling type tail-stock unclamp, G02,G03,
          G30,G31,G32,G33,G34,G35 commnd was designated.
       7->In self-travelling type tail-stock unclamp,
          axis-movement expect for W-axis was designated.
       8->W-axis order was performed by the state that there was
          not tail-stock in backplace edge, or there was not
          X-axis in plus limit, or self-travelling type tail-stock
          was unclamp, or main-spindle was not hung-up.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)The tailstock body connected state is established
         although it is actually not connected due to faulty EC 
         input signals.
       2)Operation error
       Program Example:
         :
         M189
         G02  X100  Z50  I1  F10
         :
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Correct the program.
       2)Check the EC input signals
         I/O check No.27 bit6 -> tailstock connection 
         confirmation
         I/O check No.27 bit7 -> tailstock disconnection 
         confirmation
       <For the simple tow-along tailstock specification>
         I/O check No.27 bit7 -> tailstock disconnection 
         confirmation
         (ON when disconnected, OFF when connected)
       3)If the code 3 appears, use the pulse handle for axis
         feed while the tow-along tailstock is connected.
       4)After canceling the Y-axis control mode, issue the
         tow-along tailstock connection command.
       5)After tow-along tailstook concatenaion is separated,
         a home position instruction is performed.
       [Related Specifications]Programmable tailstock

1262W-axis plus variable limit over
       Tow-along tailstock exceeds the W-axis plus variable 
       limit.
       [Object]AXIS, SYSTEM
       [Code]
       1->During operation using programmed commands
       2->During automatic returning to the joint point in
          manual operation intervention mode
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       W-axis limit has been set so that the tow-along tailstock
       joint position will be outside the soft-limit position.
       [Measures to Take]
       Shift the W-axis limit position outside if possible. 
       If such setting is not allowed, operate the turret
       manually  and carefully to connect the tailstock so that
       interference will not occur.
       [Related Specifications]Programmable tailstock

       gauging cycle.

       surface during this feed mode.
       [Object]SYSTEM

       [Measures to Take]

       whether the programmed target point and the actual workpiece
       position coincide each other.)
       Related Specification:Gauging cycle specification
1307Sensor no touch

       workpiece during execution of the G30 work gauging cycle.
       The sensor failed to contact the workpiece surface when
       it was fed from the approach point to the imaginary target
       point. Or, the sensor touched a turret other than the one
       on which gauging operation is to be carried out.
       [Object]
        SYSTEM
       [Code]
        1->During execution of the G30,
           the sensor of other-turret has touched.
        2->In the G30-order, waiting-time of sensor-state
       10->During execution of the G30 for diagonal direction,
           the sensor did not come in contact.
       The under code is unusually occured.
       10000->Sensor was touch. But NC has not get the skip-data.
       20000->NC had not get skip-data of X-axis or Z-axis.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]

        (Check whether the programmed target point and the actual
         workpiece position coincide each other.)
       [Related Specification]

1309Sensor protect
       After touching, the sensor moved over the preset distance
       Or, the turret directly hit the protection limit before
       it touches the sensor.
       preset distance:OPTIONAL PARAMETER (GAUGING)
       		Sensor protection distance
       [Object]AXIS
       [Code]Sensor input number
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Parameter setting error:The value set at the parameter
         (long word) No. 24 is too small compared with the
        feedrate in the gauging cycle.
       2)Program error, operation error:An attempt is made to
         execute the program in which the sensor is brought into
         contact with the object in cycles other than the gauging
         cycle.  Or the similar operation is attempted.
       3)Contact failure of slip ring
       4)Defective sensor element
       5)Chartering occurs depending on the machining condition.
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Reset the alarm in MANUAL mode by turning ON the emergency
         limit release switch in the control box and take the
         turret away from the touch setter using the pulse handle.
         When the turret moves out of the stroke end limit, turn
         OFF the emergency limit release switch.
       2)Set a proper value at parameter (long word) No. 24, or
         reduce the feedrate in the gauging cycle.
       3)Correct the program so that the sensor is not brought
         into contact with the object in cycles other than the 
         gauging cycle.
       4)Check the slip ring.
       5)Change the sensor element.
       6)Eliminate chartering during machining.
         If chartering cannot be eliminated, change the parameter
         MC USER PARAMETER (MEASUREMENT)
         Touch setter alarm check ineffect. at retract.
          0->Sensor contact (or limit switch input) is always
             monitored.
          1->Sensor contact (or limit switch input) is monitored
             only in gauging cycle.

1323YS axis position
       Except for Y-axis mode, though YS axis place was not in 
       turning position of system parameter, they went along axis
       movement command.
       Except for Y-axis mode, though YS axis place is not in YS
       axis carriage return place, they went along axis movement
       command (YS axis carriage return positioning specification)
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)The system parameter data for specifying YS-axis spindle
         center position is changed.
       2)After installation of NC software, axis movement was
         attempted before setting the system parameter data for
         YS-axis spindle center position.
       3)In YS axis carriage return positioning specification, 
         after YS axis carriage return place was changed, they
         went along axis movement command by the state which is
         not in YS axis carriage return place.
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Change the system parameter data to the original data.
         Or, bring the YS-axis to the newly set spindle center
         position by executing G138 (Y-axis mode ON) and G136 
         (Y-axis mode OFF).
         If the machine is provided with home position function
         and ATC unit, specify G21 (home position command) HP=4,5
         to return the saddle to the return point before issuing
         the axis movement command again.
       2)Set the system parameter data for YS-axis spindle center
         position.
       3)In YS axis carriage return positioning specification,
         Y-axis mode ON/OFF is performed. 
         Or, in order that present YS axis place results in a
         carriage return place, YS axis carriage return place
         is modified.

       from a position-order of NC.

       of NC-axis to FD by the attachment-document.
1338LOAD MONITOR W over load
       While the load monitor W function is activated, the load
       ratio of X-axis/Z-axis or Z-axis/X-axis exceeds the limit
       value. In the automatic mode, each of the programmed
       monitoring sections is controlled by the limit value S.
       The value obtained by the following formula exceeded the
       limit value S.
       VWMON[*]=1 (Z-axis torque command value/X-axis torque
       command value)*100 (%)
       VWMON[*]=1 (X-axis torque command value/Z-axis torque
       command value)*100 (%)
       [Object]SYSTEM, AXIS
       [Code]Load monitor W supervising part No. in hexadecimal
1339Door Interlock Reset
       On the machine intended for CE marking, when the state of
       servo off by door-open returned to the state of servo on
       by door-close, the following conditions are not met.
       1)In C-axis control, the position of Main spindle  is at
         least 0.36 (equivalent to 0.5mm) away from the switch
         OFF position.
       2)The spindle or M-tool spindle in the state of synchronized
         rotation, or flat turning is at least 0.36 (equivalent to
         0.5mm) away from the switch OFF position.
       [Object]SYSTEM, M-TOOL SPINDLE
1345G21 impossible
       Axis movement to the tool change position G21 is issued
       without satisfying the conditions for executing the command. 
       (G21 command is also issued in execution of ATC macro
       command G171 and M321.)
       [Code]X
       1->There are not a present place at the time of an
          instruction of G21 HP=1,2,3 and the translocation target
          place which has set on system parameter within movable
          range limit 1. Or,a turret index state has resulted in 
          the following state.
        HP=1 .... Turret is not indexed to ATC position.
       	   LB15II/LB35II-MATC-Y Turret T2-T4 T6-T8
       	   LU45-MATC-Y Turret T2
       	   MacTurn Turret T1
        HP=2 .... Turret is not indexed to ATC position .
       	   LB15II/LB35II-MATC-Y Turret T5
       	   LU45-MATC-Y turret T3
       	   MacTurn Turret T3
        HP=3 .... T1 is not indexed to ATC position 
       	   on LB15II/LB35II-M
       	   ATC-Y and LU45-MATC-Y turret.
       3->G21 was issued without opening the shutter.
       5->There is not the translocation target place that there
          are not a present place at the time of G21 HP=4,5
          instructions and the translocation target place which
          has set on system parameter within movable range limit
          1 within stroke end limit.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)There is an error in tool change position data or working
         range limit 1 setting data. The G21 HP=* command was 
         given after correcting only the tool change position
         data or working range limit 1 setting data.
       2)With HP = 1, the L-tool mounted station is indexed to
         the tool change position. With HP = 2, the facing tool 
         mounted station is indexed to the tool change position.
         (With MacTurn,M-tool mounted station is indexed to the
          tool change position.)
         With HP = 3,side machining tool is indexed to the tool
         change position.
         If the turret station having the tool type corresponding
         to G21 HP=* is not indexed to the ATC position, this
         alarm occurs.
         Satisfy the turret indexing conditions before issuing
         G21 HP=* command.
       3)G21 HP=* command cannot be issued without opening the
         shutter Issue the shutter open command before issuing 
         G21 HP=* command.
1347STM time over
       The STM operation time exceeded the parameter-set time.
       [Parameter] OPTIONAL PARAMETER (CYCLE TIME OVER CHECK)
       	     STM time over timer (0.1s)
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]Parameter-set time in hexadecimal
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)The NC received no answer to the STM command being
         executed when this alarm occurred.
       Program Example:
          :
         M03 M42 S1000 T0303
          :
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Display the check screen to see if the input signal is
         sent in answer to the STM command executed on occurrence
         of the alarm. If two or more commands are given, give
         the commands one by one in MDI operation to find out
         which STM command causes the alarm.
       2)If "0" is set at the OPTIONAL PARAMETER (CYCLE TIME OVER
         CHECK) Cycle/STM time over alarm level,
         the alarm B 2295 STM time over occurs instead of this 
         alarm.
1348Cycle time over
       One cycle time (from start to M02 or M30) exceeded the
       parameter-set time.
       [Parameter]
       OPTIONAL PARAMETER (CYCLE TIME OVER CHECK)
        Cycle time over timer (s)
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)The part program has a long machining time. Or, the part
         program failed to end because a programmed operation was
         not completed.
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Review the machining time in the part program or check
         the machining operations.
       2)if "0" is set at the OPTIONAL PARAMETER (CYCLE TIME OVER
         CHECK) Cycle/STM time over alarm level.
         the alarm C 3206 Cycle time over occurs instead of this
         alarm.

       Concerning the optical measure within a machine specification,
       ERROR signal changed on ON -> OFF in G30 cyclic practices.
       When a power supply of an optical measure within a machine
       sensor was turned on by a manually operated operational
       mode condition, ERROR signal became "OFF".

1367NC Tailstock advance error 
       Out advance of the NC tailstock.
       Concerning Sub spindle-tailstock Control specification,
       out advance of the NC tailstock.
       Concerning W axis Cut-tailstock Control specification,
       out advance of the NC tailstock.
       [Code]
       1->When the command position(CON)does not reach the
          command torque before entering the sizing position
          area1,the command torque is generated within the
          tailstock quill expand/shrink Time.
       2->The torque higher than the set thrust is generated
          when the current position(APA) is moved to the +side
          viewed from the sizing position area2.
          the tailstock to the sizing position was ordered before 
          more than  the approach position.
       3->The toraue exceeding the threshold is generated
          when the tailstock moves or the time constant(T1+T2)*
          1.25+48 msec from the approach position or movement
          start position.
       4->The current position is not within the sizing position
          area while the tailstock is in sizing position status.
       5->The torque higher than the set thrust is generated
          after lower.
       6->The torrue over for the ball screw Inertia.
       7->Real thrust is outside the tolerance of the instruction
          thrust.
       8->Difference between sizing position and current position
          values has exceeded the allowable limit.
       9->When the tailstock wasn't in A position,
          the sizing command in position B was ordered.
       10->The motor torque came off from the threshold
           by 'work position state'.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       A workpiece shorter than the required one is mounted.
       [Measures to Take]
       Re-positon the tailstock closer to the workpiece.

1509The Between the turret interfered
       The interference of Between the turret (The cover part 
       contains it) was detected with two saddle machine or three saddle
       machine. 
       This alarm approximates by rectangular shape to project 
       the turret shape to the XZ plane, and detects the interference 
       of Between the turret. 
       This alarm is not detected while manual mode and 
       manual interrupting mode.
       [Character string]
       None
       [Code]
       1->A turret and B turret interfered.
       2->A turret and B turret cover (only ZB moves) interfered.
       3->A turret cover (Only ZA moves) and B turret interfered.
       4->A turret and C turret interfered.
       5->A turret and C turret cover (only ZC moves) interfered.
       6->A turret cover (Only ZA moves) and C turret interfered.
       7->C turret and B turret interfered.
       8->C turret and B turret cover (only ZB moves) interfered.
       9->C turret cover (Only ZC moves) and B turret interfered.
       [Expected faulty point]
       Mistake of NC program instruction
       [Treatment measures]
       Please confirm the NC program on A saddle side and B saddle side 
       and C saddle side of the part where the alarm is generated. 
       This alarm might be actually generated when not interfering 
       because this alarm detects interference by the rectangular 
       approximation shape of the XZ plane for safety. 
       In that case, when it instructs the NC program of the part 
       (A saddle side or B saddle side or C saddle side) in M867
       (CAS function release), this alarm is not detected.
       However, please drive in that case after it confirms it enough.

1511SPM contour control cannot execute 
       Super-NURBS control was attempted without satisfying the 
       conditions for executing the control. 
       [Index] 
        None 
       [Character-string] 
        None 
       [Code] XYY
        X=1:NURBS interpolation processing and the other function 
            generation processing were attempted at the same time.
          YY:States of the other commands when NURBS interpolation 
       .     processing was attempted
       .   bit0->positioning command (G00) is specified at the time.
       .   bit1->Linear interpolation (G01) is specified at the time.
       .   bit2->Arc interpolation or helical cutting (G02/G03) is 
       .	  specified at the same time.
       .   bit3->Dwell (G04) is specified at the same time.
       .   bit4->Manual shift amount cancel is specified at the same time.
       .   bit7->Tolerance control mode ON is specified at the same time.
       [Cause] 
        NC control software design error
         X=F:Return to the middle of NURBS block was attempted by 
       .     the return search function.
       .   YY=01->Option code MX was specified.
       .   YY=02->Option code MY was specified.
       .   YY=03->Option code MZ was specified.
       .   YY=04->Option code TS was specified.
       [Measures to Take] 
        The above option codes for returning to the middle of NURBS 
        block by return search cannot be used. Perform return search 
        without specifying these option codes.
        XYY=200:Teaching mode was detected under the control by 
       .	 Super-NURBS.
       [Measures to Take] 
        Turn off the teaching mode. Super-NURBS control is impossible 
        during the teaching mode.

1520Synchronous error limit over

       [Character-string]
        None

        by hexadecimal notation.
       [Probable Faulty Location]

          or the brake has Failed
        In the case of 2: 
          The master or slave axis was overloaded during operation 
          or the servo has failed.
       [Measures to Take]
        In the case of 1:
          Correct using the pulse handle set to X1 in the synchronized 
          error correction mode. 
          Then, exit the mode and press RESET.
        In the case of 2: 
          Turn the power off and then on again.

       torque has exceeded the set limit before the loader axis
       reaches point D where deceleration starts.

       the torque skip occurs.
       In a torque limit check instruction, a torque value exceeded
       set data in a transfer to target position + L.
       [Code]

       2->A loader axis has arrive at "target point + L" before
          torque limit exceeded.
       3->Concerning torque limit check function, while axis
          reached target position + L, a torque value exceeded
          set data.

       1)Setting error of parameter (torque monitor delay time)
       2)Setting error for arguments in the G22 block
       3)Setting error for arguments in the G23 block

1707Stroke end over
       An axis has hit the stroke end limit.Or the axis move over
       storke end limit.
       [Code]
       None->The turret has hit the stroke end limit by X- or Z-axis
             command.
       1->During Y-axis movement on the machine with Y-axis function,
          the X-axis hit the stroke end limit.
       2->An axis hit the stroke end limit by M273 HP command (home
          position command within the stroke end limits).
       3->The work rest has hit the stroke end limit by W-axis
          command.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1->Operation error, programming error
       2->Setting error of soft-limit positions(positive/negative).
          (The soft-limit position is set outside the stroke end
       limit
           position.)
       3->Check the stroke end limit switches.
          (Is it turned on by chips or other foreign matter?)
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Push the reset button in the manual mode while turning on
       the
         emergency limit release switch on the control box, then move
         the turret away from the emergency limit position by
       rotating
         the pulse handle.
       2)After the emergency limit switch has been released, turn off
         the emergency limit release switch in the original position
         and reset the soft-limit position.
       3)In the case of new LT control specification, it is moved an
         axis in the direction which goes away from stroke end limit.

       end limit cancel switch on.Or an operation mode other than

       mode is selected.
       [Code]

       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Operation error
       [Measures to Take]

         the manual mode, then press the reset button to reset the
         alarm.
       2)Turn off the travel limit release switch.

1714S.M command asynchronous
       Under simultaneous four-axis control mode, S or M command
       provided with constant cutting speed code does not match
       between turret A and B for 2-saddle specification.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       Character-string:Coordinate system for G140, G141, or G142
       [Code]
       1->Mismatch of constant cutting speed codes (G96 and G97)
       2->Mismatch of turret selection commands (G110 and G111)
       3->Mismatch of S commands
       4->Mismatch of spindle rotation commands (M03, M04 and M05)
       5->Mismatch of spindle drive gear range commands
          (M40 through M44)
       6->Mismatch of M00 and M01
       7->Mismatch of M19 command
       8->Mismatch of M110 and M109
       9->M271, M272 instructions are different.
       10->M371, M372 instructions are different.
       11->M142, M143 instructions are different.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Mismatching S and/or M code command in simultaneous four-axis
       cut program.
       Program Example:
       Turret A
        G13
        N100 G00 X500 Z500
        N101 M41 M03 S100 P10
             ^^^     ^^^^
       Turret B
        G14
        N200 G00 X500 Z500
        N201 M42 M03  S500 P10
             ^^^      ^^^^
       [Measures to Take]
       Correct the program.
       Example
       In the program above, change the commands in N201 sequence as
       indicated below:
        N201 M41 M03 S100 P10
             ^^^     ^^^^
       Always designate the same S and M code commands at both
       turrets.
       [Related Specifications]
       2-saddle specification
1715Spindle revolution over
       The spindle drive motor rotated at a speed higher than the
       commanded speed.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1) Pulse generator PG
       2) Spindle drive motor
       3) FCP board
       4) Max speed command by G50 (If the specified spindle speed
          exceeds the max speed specified by G50, the max speed is
          automatically selected as the spindle speed.)
       5) Gear selection (low/high speed selection by motor coil
          switching) M40 to M44
1716M03/M04 change
       The spindle reverse rotation command M04 is designated while
       the spindle is rotating in the forward direction, or the
       spindle forward rotation command M03 is designated while the
       spindle is rotating in the reverse direction.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]
       1->The spindle reverse rotation command M04 is designated
          while the spindle is rotating in the forward direction, or
          the spindle forward rotation command M03 is designated
       while
          the spindle is rotating in the reverse direction.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Program error
       Program Example:
          :
         M03
         M04
          :
       (Direct switching from M03 to M04)
       [Measures to Take]
       Before switching the spindle rotation from forward (M03) to
       reverse (M04), stop the spindle first by designating M05. When
       changing the spindle rotation direction from reverse (M04) to
       forward (M03), also stop the spindle once by designating M05.

       LS have come to be unmatched.

       1->While the spindle is rotating, commanded spindle speed
          range gear and the output from the spindle speed range gear
          position LS have come to be unmatched.
       2->The spindle speed range gear position LS did not accord
          with the spindle speed range gear order, after the spindle
          speed range gear selection command was retried.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       LS setting error
1720Gear command
       Gear range selection command (M40 through M44) (M242 through
       M241) not acceptable to the machine is designated.  An attempt
       was made to change the spindle speed range gear (from M31 to
       M40 through M44, or from M40 through M44 to M31) while the
       spindle is rotating. (M31 ... super low speed range
       (optional))
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]Gear range selection command
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
         Operation error
       Operation Example:
         M43 and/or M44 is specified although the machine is the
         two-spindle speed range specification.
1721Gear neutral
       The spindle rotation command (M03, M04) is designated while
       the
       spindle drive gears are in neutral.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]
       1->The spindle rotation command is designated while the
          spindle drive gears are in neutral.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Operation error
       [Measures to Take]
       Select the spindle speed gear range other than neutral (M40)
       first, then specify the spindle rotation command.
1722Spindle orientation gear neutral
       The spindle drive gear is in the neutral position when the
       spindle orientation command (M19) is designated.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Program error
       2)Operation error
       Program Example:
         The gear range selection command is not designated before
       the
         spindle orientation command (M19), or the spindle gear range
         neutral command is designated before it.
       Operation Example:
         In the MDI mode, M19 is executed while the gear range is in
         the neutral position.
1723Spindle interference distance
       1)ZA axis or ZB axis moved to the position where distance
         between ZA axis and ZB axes become smaller than setting
       value
         of parameter long word No. 53 concerning new LT control.
       2)ZB axis moved to the position which becomes smaller than
         setting value of parameter long word No. 56 by the condition
         whose XA axis and XB axis are not together concerning new LT
         control on Plus variable limit.
       3)By the Spindlehead interlock specification, Z axis moved to
         the position which becomes smaller than setting value of
         parameter long word No. 57 by the condition whose X axis is
       on Plus variable limit.
       [Code]
       1->A case of mention above 1)
       2->A case of mention above 2)
       3->A case of mention above 3)
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Incorrect parameter long word No.53, 56, 57 setting.
       2)Operation or program error.
1724VAC spindle synchronous condition
       Any of the following conditions is not satisfied when the
       spindle synchronized control command (M151/M150) is
       designated.
       Assume that the A-spindle is controlled in synchronization
       with
       the B-spindle rotation.
       1)The spindle rotation command for the A-spindle is not
         activated.
       2)An S command for the A-spindle is not activated.
         Any of the following conditions is not satisfied when the
         spindle synchronized control ON command (M151) is
       designated.
       3)Chuck on the A-spindle is not clamped.
       4)The spindle rotation command for the B-spindle is not
         activated.
       5)An S command for the B-spindle is not activated.
       6)Fixed-speed rotation signal for the B-spindle is ON.
       7)The A-spindle gear is not in neutral.
       8)The B-spindle gear is not in neutral.
       9)The C-axis is not connected in the both A- and B-spindles.
       10)The B-spindle is not selected.
       11)The spindle speed range in which synchronized rotation is
          possible is present for both the A- and B-spindles.
       12)When the B-spindle is rotating, the B-spindle speed must be
          lower than the A-spindle speed.
          The following condition is not satisfied when the spindle
          synchronized control is OFF.
       13)The chuck on the B-spindle is not clamped.
       14)The thing that mutual Main spindle is not in extreme low
          speed rotation mode either.
       15)The thing that mutual Main spindle is not in Main spindle
          low speed acceleration mode either.
       16)Both spindle's chucks are not closed.
       17)A synchronous rotation command was issued with the second
          headstock not at the lowered position.
       18)APA is effective in the both A- and B-spindles.
       19)The spindle synchronized rotation phasing cancel command
          (M210) must be executed, When the both clamped IL cancel
          command(M883) execute.
       20)The C-axis is not clamped in the both A- and B-spindles.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code] The number (hexadecimal) of each of the above
       conditions
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Program error
       Program Example:
          :            :
         G13          G141
         M40          M110
         M151          :
          :           M151
                       :
       [Measures to Take]
       Correct the program.
          :            :
         G13          G141
         M41<-Changed M110
         M151          :
          :    Added->M109
                      M151
                       :

1729C-axis advance
       During the execution of the C-axis connection (M110), C-axis
       retraction end limit remains ON for more than 10[s] when
       C-axis advance command is designated.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)For the advance output signal in the C-axis connection,
         the mechanical system and the electrical system (EC) fail to
         operate normally.
       2)Defective LS confirming the retraction end.
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Check and adjust the mechanical and electrical parts related
         with the C-axis advance movement.
       2)Check the signal input from the retraction end confirmation
         LS.
1730Turret clamp or position
       The turret clamp signal is turned off during axis movement
       [function generation] (except manual operation).
       Or a mismatch between tool numbers has continued for more
       than 1[s].
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]XYY
       X:
       None->Mismatch between programmed and actual tool numbers
       1->During axis movement [function generation], the turret
          clamp confirmation signal went out.
       2->A mismatch between the programmed tool number and the
       actual
          tool number is found after the turret has been clamped
       3->A cutting feed command is issued while the NC turret is
          unclamped, and the turret is not clamped within 500[ms]
          after designation of the command.
       4->The command of cutting-feed was performed by the state that
          was not "M-tool spindle edge angle" when L-tool or sensor
          is registered with present-tool.
       5->The rapid feed or manual jog feed or puluse handle feed
          command is issued, while the NC turret is not clamped and
          turret index motor's servo is OFF.
       7->Turret positioning is not finished.
       YY:Hexadecimal number of designated tool number
       FFFFFFFF:A tool index command other than T1 was issued when
                an NC round table or stationary turret was mounted.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)An abnormality occurred in the turret clamp confirmation
         limit switch, turret-related wiring, or the turret index
         limit switch.
       2)T-axis position encoder offset value
       [Measures to Take]
       [Code]X=None->Check the EC input related with the tool number.
       [Code]X=1, 4 or 5->Check the clamp confirmation LS.
       [Code]X=2->Check the EC input related with the tool number;
                 adjust the turret index solenoid when the turret
                 overpasses the designated position.

1733Tool number input
       The tool number of the turret is not input as specified.
       * The turret tool number input signals differ depending on
       machine models.  Refer to the description below.
       1)LC, LH, LS series
         I/O check NO.28 INPUT bit 0 to bit 7
         to the tool numbers 1 to 8.
         I/O check NO.37 INPUT bit 0 to bit 3
         to the tool numbers 9 to 12.
       2)LS30N, LH35N, LH55N (Indexing by rotary switch),LCS15/25
         (Index position check by limit switch or proximity switch)
         See Table 1.
       Relations between Tool Numbers and Input Bits
       Table 1
         I/O check NO.28 INPUT bit 0 to bit 7
        T  b7 b6 b5 b4 b3 b2 b1 b0
        1   0  0  0  0  0  0  1  1
        2   0  0  0  0  1  0  0  1
        3   0  0  0  0  0  1  0  1
        4   0  0  0  1  0  0  0  1
        5   0  0  0  1  0  1  1  1
        6   0  0  0  1  1  1  0  1
        7   0  0  0  0  1  1  1  1
        8   0  0  0  1  1  0  1  1
        9   0  1  0  1  0  0  1  1
       10   0  1  0  0  1  1  0  1
       11   0  0  1  0  1  1  0  1
       12   0  0  1  1  0  0  1  1
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]XXX:Tool No. input when the alarm has occurred
       (hexadecimal)
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Turret related limit switches
       2)Proximity switch clearance
       3)Turret wiring

1747Tailstock quill advance answer

       has been executed.

          command has been executed.

          input within setting value of parameter  after the
          tailstock spindle advance cmmand has been executed.

       Faulty adjustments of tailstock spindle in-position
       confirmation LS

       that they come ON at the same time when the tailstock spindle
       is advanced until it touches the workpiece.
1748Tailstock quill advance over
       The tailstock spindle has over-advanced, exceeding the advance
       end limit position.
       [Code]
       1->The tailstock spindle over-advanced to actuate the
          over-advance confirmation LS
       2->The tailstock spindle over-advanced to
       the in-position LS was OFF.
       3->In the case of NC tailstock spcification, the tailstock
          spindle over-advanced and the workpiece hold confirmation
          LS turned OFF.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)A workpiece shorter than the required one is mounted.
         (Operation error)
       2)The axis hit the overtravel limit switch before touching the
         workpiece because the initial tailstock position is too far
         from the workpiece.
       3)The tailstock advance command was issued without mounting
         any workpiece. (Operation error)
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Re-position the tailstock closer to the workpiece, or adjust
         the dog position.
       2)Designate the tailstock spindle advance command only after
         setting a workpiece in the chuck.

1754Coupling device illegal
       An abnormality is detected with the device coupled with the
       machine.
       [Code]
       1->Input signals from the loader (Loader Continuous Operation
          and No Loader Interference) turned OFF at the same time
          (for loader interface types).
       2->In the case of stacker crane I/F specification, if the APC
          operation OK signal turned OFF during APC operation in the
          ON state of the SYSTEM LINK switch.
          Or, M934 command was designated in the APC operation OK
          signal OFF and the ON state of the SYSTEM LINK switch.
          However, when "1" is set at item "Reverse input APC start
          OK (1:Stops by input ON)" of the MC user parameter ROBOT
          LOADER I/F, this alarm occurs by the APC operation OK
          signal ON.
       3->On the APC interface type C specifications, the APC illegal
          input signal turned OFF.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Coupling devices (loader and robot)
       2)The emergency stop button at a coupling device has been
         activated.
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Recover the coupling devices and reset.
       2)The emergency stop button at a coupling device has been
         activated.
       [Related Specifications]
       Robot/Loader interface
       Stacker crane interface
