1760Revolution tool M13/M14 change
       In the automatic or MDI mode of operation,
       1)Reverse rotation command is designated while the M-tool
         spindle is rotating in the forward direction.
       2)Forward rotation command is designated while the M-tool
         spindle is rotating in the reverse direction.
       Note:  These commands are ignored in the manual mode.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]1
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Program error
       2)Wrong command input in the MDI mode
       Program Example:
         N100 M13  M-tool spindle FWD
         N101 M14  M-tool spindle REV
       Operation Example:
       In MDI mode, a rotating direction opposite to the current
       rotating direction was specified as a rotary tool rotation
       command.
       [Measures to Take]
         N100 M13
         N101 M12
         N102 M14
1761Revolution tool gear match
       Mismatch between the gear range command and the position of
       gear range setting limit switches occurs while the M-tool
       spindle is rotating.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Code]1
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Faulty EC input signals
          I/O check NO.29 INPUT bit 8 (iMA241)---M241
          I/O check NO.29 INPUT bit 9 (iMA242)---M242
       2)Error in adjustments of gear match confirmation limit switch
       [Measures to Take]
       Check the related EC input signals.
1762Revolution tool gear command
       The M-tool spindle gear command values are checked with the
       machine specifications.  If an improper value is detected,
       this alarm occurs.
       [Object]SYSTEM
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Program error
       Program Example:
       The M-tool spindle speed change command is given for the
       machine which has single M-tool spindle speed specification.
       The M-tool spindle speed change command other than M241 and
       M242 is given for the machine which has the two M-tool spindle
       specification.
       [Measures to Take]
       1)For single-speed model:
         The spindle speed change command is not allowed.
       2)For two-speed model:
         Only M241 and M242 are allowed.

       confirmation limit switch is out of position or faulty.

       of position or faulty.
       2)For the door of mechanical locking type, a door open/close
       confirmation limit switch is faulty.

       2)Change the faulty limit switch for mechanical locking door
       open/close confirmation.

1773Door Interlock Reset
       On the machine intended for CE marking, the magnet switches in
       high-precision VAC and servo amplifier are turned off by
       opening the door and turned on by pressing the reset switchor
       closing the door.When the switches change their status from
       OFF
       to ON, the following conditions are not met.
       1)The feed axis (including the spindle under C-axis control)
       is
         at least 0.5[mm] away from the position detected when the
         magnet switch was turned off.
       2)The spindle or M-tool spindle in the state of orient-stop,
         synchronized rotation, or flat turning is at least 0.36.
         (equivalent to 0.5[mm]) away from the switch OFF position.
       [Object]SYSTEM, AXIS, M-TOOL SPINDLE

       other

         switch.

       and answer of door opening and shutting has not returned.

       2->No signal is output to confirm that the front door is
          closed.

          open.
       4->No signal is output to confirm that the ceiling door is
          closed.
       5->No signal is output to confirm that the APC door is open.
       6->No signal is output to confirm that the APC door is close.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)The front or ceiling door does not correctly work.
       2)A faulty limit switch at the front or ceiling door.
       3)An object or human body is pinched by the front or ceiling
         door.
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Adjust the door so that it will smoothly move.
       2)Adjust the limit switch so that it will correctly function
       or
       change it with a new one.
       3) Remove the object or human body pinched by the door.
       [Related functions]
       Automatic doors
       Ceiling door

       1)Check the operation procedure.
       2)Replace the ENABLE button on the machine with a new one.
1804Safety speed monitor output illegal
        The ER-PW signal was not correctly transmitted from the speed
       monitor to the loader power unit (MIP unit) due to a hardware
       circuit failure, e.g. fused relay.  This alarm occurs when the
       following two input signals are kept ON or OFF for 0.5 second
       or longer.
       Speed monitor alarm/(OGL)      iSVLRER/  I.053D
       Speed monitor alarm (OGL)      iSVLRER   I.053C
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)A hardware circuit failure
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Check the hardware circuit from the speed monitor to the
         loader power unit (MIP unit).
1805Teaching panel enabling illegal
        The ENABLE button on the teaching panel kept ON for 5
       seconds or longer when it does not need to be operated (for
       CE-marked OR robot/OGL loader types) or the hardware circuit
       of that button was failed (for OR robot types only).
       [Code]
       None->The ENABLE button on the teaching panel kept ON for 5
             seconds or longer in robot/loader teaching mode with the
             safety guard locked and the robot/loader running.
       1->The ENABLE button on the teaching panel has a hardware
          circuit failure, e.g. fused relay (for CE-marked OR robot
          types).  This alarm occurs when the following two input
          signals are kept ON or OFF for 0.5 second or longer.
               ENABLE button (on TP)/      iCELRENF
           I.0532
               ENABLE button (on TP)       iCELRENB
           I.0538
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)An operation error
       2)The ENABLE button on the teaching panel is faulty.
       3)A hardware circuit failure
       [Measures to Take]
       1)Check the operation procedure.
       2)Replace the ENABLE button on the teaching panel with a
         new one.
       3)Replace faulty hardware circuit components with new ones.

1829Sp. oil air lub. air pressure error
        The air pressure for oil-air spindle lubrication is too low.
        A pressure error of air continued more than 30 seconds at
       the time of output the air.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1) Air pump or piping
       2) Pressure switch
       3) Inferiority of oil-air plumbing.
       4) Inferiority of oil-air pressure PS.
       [Measures to Take]
       1) Change the air unit with a new one.
       2) Change the air pressure switch with a new one.
       3) Inspection of oil-air plumbing.
       4) Exchange of oil-air pressure PS.
1830SP. oil air lub. oil level error
        The oil level in the oil-air spindle lubrication tank is too
       low.
        A oil-air lubricant liquid surface fall condition continued
       more than 3 seconds.
       [Code]
       1-> A M SP.oil-air lubricant liquid surface fall condition
           continued more than 3 seconds.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1) An insufficient oil-air spindle lubricant level
       2) A faulty oil-air spindle lubricant level sensor
       [Measures to Take]
       1) Supply oil to the oil-air lubrication unit for spindle.
       2) Change the sensor for monitoring the oil level of the
          oil-air lubrication unit with a new one.
1831Sp. oil air lub. oil pressure error
        The oil pressure for oil-air spindle lubrication is wrong.
       [Code]
       1->The oil-air lubricant pressure did not rise to 1.2 MPa
          within 60 seconds after the oil-air spindle lubrication
          output signal turned ON.
       2->The oil-air lubricant pressure did not fall to 0.8 MPa
          before the oil-air spindle lubrication output off-time was
          elapsed.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1) A faulty pressure relief valve, clogged filter or pipe,
          or poor pump operation
       2) A faulty oil-air pressure monitor switch
       [Measures to Take]
       1) Change the oil-air lubrication unit with a new one.
       2) Replace the pressure switch with a new one.

1861Stroke end over

       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       Setting error of soft-limits
       [Corrective action]

         in the electrical control box and select the manual mode
         for the robot/loader. After that reset the robot/loader and
         move the robot/loader axis away from the travel limit
       switch.
       2)After moving the robot/loader axis away from the travel
       limit
         switch, turn OFF the robot/loader axis limit emergency
       release
         switch. Then, set the soft-limits correctly.

1872Safety fence interlock
       The safety fence was opened during loader (robot) operation.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       The safety fence is fastened by the electromagnet lock and
       cannot be opened during loader (robot) operation.
       Therefore, electromagnetic lock switch should be faulty or its
       wiring is  disconnected.
       [Measures to Take]
       Check the electromagnetic lock switch and its wiring on the
       safety fence.

       loadersoperation.

          start to move during the signal of area sensor is OFF.
       2->The signal of area sensor is OFF during loader axis
          running by manual when front door is not close condition.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
        The magnetic (mechanical) lock switch must be faulty or have
       a cut wire as the front door on the machine should be kept
       closed by the magnetic (mechanical) lock switch when the OGL
       loader (OR robot) is moving.
       [Measures to Take]
        Replace the front door magnetic (mechanical) lock switch
       with a new one and check the wiring.

1881Part turnover device R clamp empty
       In program operation, there are no workpieces when the
       R-side turn-over hand close command is executed.
       If the hand close confirmation input signal goes ON while
       the turn-over hand is closing, it is judged that there are
       no workpieces.
       This alarm dose not occur with the turn-over hand close
       command executed in manual operation mode.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Program error(turn-over hand close command is specified
         although there are no workpieces.)
       2)Workpiece transfer error

       no workpieces.

1883Part turn device R advanced too far

       command is executed, the unit advanced excessively.
       If the turn-advance confirmation input signal goes ON while
       the unit is moving forward, it is judged that over-advance
       had occurred.
       This alarm dose not occur with the advance command executed
       in manual operation mode.
       [Probable Faulty Locations]
       1)Program error(advance command was executed although the
         workpiece transfer loader is not at the correct position.)
       2)Workpiece transfer position setting error

1897Lower turret drive belt torn off
        The lower turret drive belt was torn off.
1898OP panel within interference range
        The operation panel retract position signal turned OFF when
       the loader has entered or was in the machine.
       [Code]
       1->The machine operation panel is not at the retract position.
       2->The machine operation panel left the home position in
          AUTO mode with LINK mode selected and the NC unit running.
1899Safety fence status
        The safety fence opened or the peripheral equipment stopped
       for emergency with the loader in programmed or MDI operation
       mode.
       [Code]
       [Measures to Take]
       Select a loader operation mode other than programmed or
       MDI operation modes or close the safety fence or recover the
       peripheral equipment from the emergency stop.
